1d:T461,Wahoo! First 4 Figures is proud to present the high-quality PVC collectible, Mario from the beloved video game, Mario Kart which debuted in 1992. Everything you know and love about Mario is brought to life in this incredible statue. Realistic touches add depth and nuance to the smallest details - from fabric and stitching on his bright red cap to the smoke coming off of the spinning wheels of his go-kart. The go-kart itself is modeled after the classic Pipe Frame design, with lifelike parts and details.

The Collector's Edition of this statue has an expanded base with LED light-up function.
The base's design makes it appear as if Mario is speeding across the finish line! Long
lights all around the base glow a brilliant white when activated.

Comes with the following:

- Exquisitely detailed PVC statue of Mario
- Pose inspired by video game
- Round black base with finishing line and race track details
- LED function for the base (Static Mode only)
- F4F Leaflet with 500 F4F reward points included

Size: 22 cm
